  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  // The following holds because t = s[..i] + [s[i]]
  assert t == s[..i] + [s[i]];
  // Therefore Sum(t) = Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    // Using the induction hypothesis: 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1)*m
    // Adding a[k-1] preserves the bounds
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1)*m + m;
    // Simplify the right side
    assert (k-1)*m + m == k * m;
    // Therefore 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k*m
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{

  var i := 0;

    i := i + 1;
  }

  if s < m {

  } else {
    score := m;
  }

// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]); // explicit use of lemma definition
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1]; // from the definition of Sum
  assert Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert (k-1) * m + m == k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
  assert Achievable(a, m, score);
  assert forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v);
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert 0 <= 0 <= 0 * m;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).

ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
  // sum of t equals sum of the prefix plus the last element
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)

    // using the invariant from the recursive call and the property of a[k-1]
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
  }

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  // Proof by definition of Sum
  assert Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)

    i := i + 1;

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);

  }

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  // Since t = s[..i] + [s[i]], the sum property follows by definition of Sum
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    // From ValidScores we know 0 <= a[k-1] <= m
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    // Combine with the induction hypothesis
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert (k-1) * m + m == k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    // Before adding a[i], we have s == Sum(a[..i])
    SumAppend(a, i);
    // After SumAppend, we know Sum(a[..i+1]) == Sum(a[..i]) + a[i]
    assert Sum(a[..i+1]) == Sum(a[..i]) + a[i];
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  } else {
    score := m;

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]); // from invariant of Sum
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
  assert t == s[..i] + [s[i]];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
    assert 0 <= 0 <= 0 * m;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert (k-1) * m + m == k * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{

  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{

    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert t == s[..i] + [s[i]]; // Added assertion to relate t and s
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]; // Added assertion to establish the sum property
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0; // Added assertion for the base case sum
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1]; // Relate sums
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m; // Use induction hypothesis
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= (k-1) * m + a[k-1];
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= (k-1) * m + m; // Since a[k-1] <= m
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m; // Final bound
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)

    i := i + 1;

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  // `t` has length `i+1`; the last element is `s[i]`
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  // The sum of `t` is the sum of its prefix plus the last element.
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]); // from the prefix equality
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];               // from the definition of `t`
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
    assert 0 <= 0 <= 0 * m;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    // From the induction hypothesis we know the sum of the first k-1 elements.
    // The k-th element is bounded by `m`.
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    // Combine the bounds to get the desired range for the first k elements.
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert (k-1) * m + m == k * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  // By definition of sequence concatenation
  assert s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]];
  // Sum behaviour
  assert Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    // a[k-1] is in [0, m]
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    // Sum(a[..k]) = Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1]
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    // By induction hypothesis 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1)*m
    // and a[k-1] <= m, so Sum(a[..k]) <= k*m
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= (k-1)*m + m == k*m;
  }
}

  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert (k-1) * m + m == k * m; // helper assertion
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{

ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0

  requires 0 <= i < |s|

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]); // use lemma recursively
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
    assert 0 <= 0 <= 0 * m;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert (k-1) * m + m == k * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

{

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)

  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].

  requires |a| > 0

  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m

  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{

--- LLM RESPONSE (750 tokens, 5.22s) ---
<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]); // why this needs to exist for the prover
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1] by Sum;
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0; // because Sum([]) == 0
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1)*m + m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]);
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
  assert t == s[..i] + [s[i]];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= (k-1) * m + a[k-1];
    assert (k-1) * m + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert (k-1) * m + m == k * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert t == s[..i] + [s[i]];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert (k-1) * m + m == k * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..0]) <= 0 * m;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
  assert Achievable(a, m, score);
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k - 1]) <= (k - 1) * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= (k - 1) * m + m;
    assert (k - 1) * m + m == k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]

{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]);
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)

    i := i + 1;

    score := m;
  }

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0

  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]

  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]);
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];

  decreases k

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  // By definition of Sum for a sequence with one more element
  assert Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..0]) <= 0 * m;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}
